-- 鐩爣鎴愭湰琛?-- ----------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS cost_target (
    id BIGINT NOT NULL COMMENT '鐩爣鎴愭湰ID锛岄洩鑺盜D',
    tenant_id BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '绉熸埛ID',
    project_id BIGINT NOT NULL COMMENT '椤圭洰ID',
    version_no VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL COMMENT '鐗堟湰鍙?,
    version_name VARCHAR(200) NULL COMMENT '鐗堟湰鍚嶇О',
    total_target_amount DECIMAL(18,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '鐩爣鎴愭湰鎬婚',
    is_active TINYINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '鏄惁鐢熸晥鐗堟湰锛?鍚︼紝1鏄€傚悓涓€椤圭洰浠呭厑璁镐竴涓敓鏁堢増鏈?,
    approval_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'DRAFT' COMMENT '瀹℃壒鐘舵€侊細DRAFT鑽夌锛孉PPROVING瀹℃壒涓紝APPROVED宸查€氳繃锛孯EJECTED宸查┏鍥?,
    effective_date DATE NULL COMMENT '鐢熸晥鏃ユ湡',
    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'DRAFT' COMMENT '涓氬姟鐘舵€侊細DRAFT鑽夌锛孉PPROVING瀹℃壒涓紝ACTIVE宸茬敓鏁堬紝CANCELLED宸蹭綔搴?,
    created_by BIGINT NULL COMMENT '鍒涘缓浜?,
    created_time DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '鍒涘缓鏃堕棿',
    updated_by BIGINT NULL COMMENT '鏇存柊浜?,
    updated_time DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '鏇存柊鏃堕棿',
    deleted_flag TINYINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '閫昏緫鍒犻櫎锛?鍚︼紝1鏄?,
    remark TEXT NULL COMMENT '澶囨敞',
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    KEY idx_cost_target_project (project_id),
    KEY idx_cost_target_active (project_id, is_active)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='鐩爣鎴愭湰琛?

    target_amount DECIMAL(18,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '鐩爣閲戦',
    created_by BIGINT NULL COMMENT '鍒涘缓浜?,
    created_time DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '鍒涘缓鏃堕棿',
    updated_by BIGINT NULL COMMENT '鏇存柊浜?,

    remark VARCHAR(500) NULL COMMENT '澶囨敞',
    PRIMARY KEY (id),

    KEY idx_cost_target_item_subject (cost_subject_id),

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='鐩爣鎴愭湰鏄庣粏琛?

-- 1. VAR_ORDER锛堝彉鏇寸璇侊級锛歷ar_order_item 琛ㄥ凡鏈?cost_subject_id
-- ============================================================
UPDATE cost_item ci
INNER JOIN var_order_item voi ON ci.source_item_id = voi.id
SET ci.cost_subject_id = voi.cost_subject_id
WHERE ci.source_type = 'VAR_ORDER'
  AND ci.cost_subject_id IS NULL
  AND ci.deleted_flag = 0
  AND voi.cost_subject_id IS NOT NULL
2026-06-12T22:39:32.459+08:00 DEBUG 34756 --- [cgc-pms-backend] [           main] o.f.c.i.sqlscript.ParserSqlScript        : Found statement at line 26: -- ============================================================
-- 2. MAT_RECEIPT锛堟潗鏂欓獙鏀讹級锛氭槧灏勫埌 cost_subject.subject_type = '鏉愭枡'
-- ============================================================
UPDATE cost_item ci
SET ci.cost_subject_id = (
    SELECT id FROM (
        SELECT cs.id
        FROM cost_subject cs
        WHERE cs.tenant_id = ci.tenant_id
          AND cs.subject_type = '鏉愭枡'
          AND cs.status = 'ENABLE'
          AND cs.deleted_flag = 0
        ORDER BY cs.level ASC
        LIMIT 1
    ) t
)
WHERE ci.source_type = 'MAT_RECEIPT'
  AND ci.cost_subject_id IS NULL
  AND ci.deleted_flag = 0

        FROM cost_subject cs

        LIMIT 1
    ) t
)
WHERE ci.source_type = 'SUB_MEASURE'
  AND ci.cost_subject_id IS NULL
  AND ci.deleted_flag = 0

2026-06-12T22:39:32.484+08:00 DEBUG 34756 --- [cgc-pms-backend] [           main] o.flywaydb.core.internal.parser.Parser   : Parsing V27__fix_dynamic_cost_formula_backfill.sql ...
2026-06-12T22:39:32.485+08:00 DEBUG 34756 --- [cgc-pms-backend] [           main] o.f.c.i.sqlscript.ParserSqlScript        : Found statement at line 14: -- V27__fix_dynamic_cost_formula_backfill.sql
-- 寤虹瓚宸ョ▼鎬诲寘椤圭洰鍏ㄨ繃绋嬬鐞嗙郴缁?- 鍔ㄦ€佹垚鏈叕寮忎慨姝?+ backfill
-- 鏁版嵁搴擄細MySQL 8.0+
--
-- Bug 淇:
--   1. refreshSummary 鍏紡: dynamicCost = actualCost + estimatedRemainingCost锛堢Щ闄?contractLockedCost 鍙岄噸璁＄畻锛?--   2. getProjectSummary 鍏紡: 涓?refreshSummary 缁熶竴
--   3. estimatedRemainingCost = SUM(contract.currentAmount) - SUM(sub_measure.approvedAmount | approved) - SUM(mat_receipt.totalAmount | approved)
--   4. contractIncome = SUM(contract.contractAmount) + SUM(var_order.approvedAmount | direction='INCOME' AND approved)
--   5. expectedProfit = contractIncome - dynamicCost
--
-- 姝よ縼绉诲洖濉墍鏈夊巻鍙?cost_summary 琛岋紝纭繚鍙屽叕寮忕粺涓€鍚庡巻鍙叉暟鎹竴鑷淬€?
SET NAMES utf8mb4
2026-06-12T22:39:32.485+08:00 DEBUG 34756 --- [cgc-pms-backend] [           main] o.f.c.i.sqlscript.ParserSqlScript        : Found statement at line 15: SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 0
2026-06-12T22:39:32.486+08:00 DEBUG 34756 --- [cgc-pms-backend] [           main] o.f.c.i.sqlscript.ParserSqlScript        : Found statement at line 23: -- ============================================================
-- Step 1: 鍥炲～ estimated_remaining_cost銆乧ontract_income
--         骞堕噸绠?dynamic_cost銆乪xpected_profit銆乧ost_deviation
-- ============================================================
-- 浣跨敤 JOIN + 瀛愭煡璇㈣绠楅」鐩骇瀛楁锛岄伩鍏?MySQL 鍚岃〃鏇存柊瀛愭煡璇㈤檺鍒?
UPDATE cost_summary cs
JOIN (
    SELECT
        proj.tenant_id,
        proj.project_id,
        -- contractIncome = SUM(contract.contractAmount) + SUM(income var_order.approvedAmount)
        COALESCE(contract_amts.contract_amount, 0)
            + COALESCE(income_vars.income_amount, 0) AS calc_contract_income,
        -- estimatedRemainingCost = SUM(contract.currentAmount)
        --                       - SUM(sub_measure.approvedAmount | approved)
        --                       - SUM(mat_receipt.totalAmount | approved)
        COALESCE(contract_currs.current_amount, 0)
            - COALESCE(measures.measure_amount, 0)
            - COALESCE(receipts.receipt_amount, 0) AS calc_estimated_remaining
    FROM (SELECT DISTINCT tenant_id, project_id FROM cost_summary WHERE deleted_flag = 0) proj
    -- 鍚堝悓閲戦鍚堣 (contractAmount)
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT tenant_id, project_id, SUM(COALESCE(contract_amount, 0)) AS contract_amount
        FROM ct_contract WHERE deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) contract_amts
        ON proj.tenant_id = contract_amts.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = contract_amts.project_id
    -- 鍚堝悓褰撳墠閲戦鍚堣 (currentAmount)
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT tenant_id, project_id, SUM(COALESCE(current_amount, 0)) AS current_amount
        FROM ct_contract WHERE deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) contract_currs
        ON proj.tenant_id = contract_currs.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = contract_currs.project_id
    -- 鏀跺叆绫荤璇佸瀹氶噾棰濆悎璁?(direction='INCOME' AND approved)
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT tenant_id, project_id, SUM(COALESCE(approved_amount, 0)) AS income_amount
        FROM var_order
        WHERE direction = 'INCOME' AND approval_status = 'APPROVED' AND deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) income_vars
        ON proj.tenant_id = income_vars.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = income_vars.project_id
    -- 宸插鎵瑰垎鍖呰閲忓瀹氶噾棰濆悎璁?    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT tenant_id, project_id, SUM(COALESCE(approved_amount, 0)) AS measure_amount
        FROM sub_measure
        WHERE approval_status = 'APPROVED' AND deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) measures
        ON proj.tenant_id = measures.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = measures.project_id
    -- 宸插鎵规潗鏂欓獙鏀堕噾棰濆悎璁?    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT tenant_id, project_id, SUM(COALESCE(total_amount, 0)) AS receipt_amount
        FROM mat_receipt
        WHERE approval_status = 'APPROVED' AND deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) receipts
        ON proj.tenant_id = receipts.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = receipts.project_id
) calc
    ON cs.tenant_id = calc.tenant_id
    AND cs.project_id = calc.project_id
SET
    cs.estimated_remaining_cost = calc.calc_estimated_remaining,
    cs.contract_income         = calc.calc_contract_income,
    cs.dynamic_cost            = COALESCE(cs.actual_cost, 0) + calc.calc_estimated_remaining,
    cs.expected_profit         = calc.calc_contract_income - (COALESCE(cs.actual_cost, 0) + calc.calc_estimated_remaining),
    cs.cost_deviation          = (COALESCE(cs.actual_cost, 0) + calc.calc_estimated_remaining) - COALESCE(cs.target_cost, 0)
WHERE cs.deleted_flag = 0

        FROM ct_contract WHERE deleted_flag = 0

    -- 鍚堝悓褰撳墠閲戦鍚堣 (currentAmount)
    LEFT JOIN (

        FROM ct_contract WHERE deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) contract_currs

        AND proj.project_id = contract_currs.project_id
    -- 鏀跺叆绫荤璇佸瀹氶噾棰濆悎璁?(direction='INCOME' AND approved)

        FROM var_order
        WHERE direction = 'INCOME' AND approval_status = 'APPROVED' AND deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) income_vars
        ON proj.tenant_id = income_vars.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = income_vars.project_id
    -- 宸插鎵瑰垎鍖呰閲忓瀹氶噾棰濆悎璁?    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT tenant_id, project_id, SUM(COALESCE(approved_amount, 0)) AS measure_amount
        FROM sub_measure
        WHERE approval_status = 'APPROVED' AND deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) measures
        ON proj.tenant_id = measures.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = measures.project_id
    -- 宸插鎵规潗鏂欓獙鏀堕噾棰濆悎璁?    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT tenant_id, project_id, SUM(COALESCE(total_amount, 0)) AS receipt_amount
        FROM mat_receipt
        WHERE approval_status = 'APPROVED' AND deleted_flag = 0
        GROUP BY tenant_id, project_id
    ) receipts
        ON proj.tenant_id = receipts.tenant_id
        AND proj.project_id = receipts.project_id
) calc
    ON cs.tenant_id = calc.tenant_id
    AND cs.project_id = calc.project_id
SET
    cs.estimated_remaining_cost = calc.calc_estimated_remaining,
    cs.contract_income         = calc.calc_contract_income,
    cs.dynamic_cost            = COALESCE(cs.actual_cost, 0) + calc.calc_estimated_remaining,
    cs.expected_profit         = calc.calc_contract_income - (COALESCE(cs.actual_cost, 0) + calc.calc_estimated_remaining),
    cs.cost_deviation          = (COALESCE(cs.actual_cost, 0) + calc.calc_estimated_remaining) - COALESCE(cs.target_cost, 0)
WHERE cs.deleted_flag = 0
